<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:neen.html>neen</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*nn</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote"></span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:none.html>none</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:not.html>not</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:one.html>one</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote"></span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:ne.html>ne</a></i> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">n</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*<a href = vnd.unilang:ne.html>ne</a></i> + <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*ainaz</i>. <head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:neer.html>neer</a> (498)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
